saTokenControllerDescriptor\\n325: \\t\\t\\t\\trun(ctx, controllerDescriptors)\\n326: \\t\\t\\t},\\n327: \\t\\t\\tOnStoppedLeading: func() {\\n328: \\t\\t\\t\\tlogger.Error(nil, \\\"leaderelection lock.\\n334: \\tif leaderMigrator != nil {\\n335: \\t\\t// Wait for Service Account Token Controller to start before acquiring the migration lock.\\n336: \\t\\t// At this point, the main lock must have already been acquired, or the KCM process already exited.\\n337: \\t\\t// We wait for the main lock before acquiring the migration lock to prevent the situation\\n338: \\t\\t//  where KCM \\treturn nil\\n363: }\\n364: \\n365: // ControllerContext defines the context object for controller\\n366: type ControllerContext struct {\\n367: \\t// ClientBuilder will provide a client for this nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\\n416: // that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\\n417: // Any error returned will cause the controller process to ControllerContext\\n662: func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\\n663: \\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\\n664: \\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\\n665: \\n666: \\t// Always start the SA token controller ControllerContext\\n662: func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\\n663: \\tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\\n664: \\tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\\n665: \\n666: \\t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\\n667: \\t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\\n668: \\tif klog.FromContext(ctx)\\n713: \\tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\\n714: \\n715: \\tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\\n716: \\t\\tif In Kubernetes, a controller is a control loop that watches the shared\n113: state of the cluster through the apiserver and makes changes attempting to move the\n114: current state towards the desired state. All generic controllers currently use\n375: \t// object metadata - if a future controller needs access to the full object this\n376: \t// would become GenericInformerFactory and take a dynamic client.\n377: \tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory informerfactory.InformerFactory\n378: \n379: \t// ComponentConfig provides access to init options for a given controller\n380: \tComponentConfig kubectrlmgrconfig.KubeControllerManagerConfiguration\n381: \n382: \t// DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper is a RESTMapper that will defer\n383: \t// initialization of the RESTMapper until the first mapping is\n384: \t// requested.\n385: \tRESTMapper *restmapper.DeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper\n386: \n387: \t// InformersStarted is closed after all of the controllers have been initialized and are running.  After this point it is safe,\n388: \t// for an individual controller to start the shared informers. Before it is closed, they should not.\n389: \tInformersStarted chan struct{}\n390: \n391: \t// ResyncPeriod generates a duration each time it is invoked; this is so that\n392: \t// multiple controllers don't get into lock-step and all hammer the apiserver\n393: \t// with list requests simultaneously.\n394: \tResyncPeriod func() time.Duration\n395: \n396: \t// ControllerManagerMetrics provides a proxy to set controller manager specific metrics.\n397: \tControllerManagerMetrics *controllersmetrics.ControllerManagerMetrics\n398: \n399: \t// GraphBuilder gives an access to dependencyGraphBuilder which keeps tracks of resources in the cluster\n400: \tGraphBuilder *garbagecollector.GraphBuilder\n401: }\n402: \n403: // IsControllerEnabled checks if the context's controllers enabled or not\n404: func (c ControllerContext) IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor) bool {\n405: \tcontrollersDisabledByDefault := sets.NewString()\n406: \tif controllerDescriptor.IsDisabledByDefault() {\n407: \t\tcontrollersDisabledByDefault.Insert(controllerDescriptor.Name())\n408: \t}\n409: \treturn genericcontrollermanager.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor.Name(), controllersDisabledByDefault, c.ComponentConfig.Generic.Controllers)\n410: }\n411: \n412: // InitFunc is used to launch a particular controller. It returns a controller\n413: // that can optionally implement other interfaces so that the controller manager\n414: // can support the requested features.\n415: // The returned controller may be nil, which will be considered an anonymous controller\n416: // that requests no additional features from the controller manager.\n417: // Any error returned will cause the controller process to `Fatal`\n418: // The bool indicates whether the controller was enabled.\n419: type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\n420: \n421: type ControllerDescriptor struct {\n422: \tname                      string\n423: \tinitFunc                  InitFunc\n424: resources needed by the\n596: // controllers such as the cloud provider and clientBuilder. rootClientBuilder is only used for\n597: // the shared-informers client and token controller.\n598: func CreateControllerContext(ctx context.Context, s *config.CompletedConfig, rootClientBuilder, clientBuilder clientbuilder.ControllerClientBuilder) (ControllerContext, error) {\n599: \t// Informer transform to trim ManagedFields for memory efficiency.\n600: \ttrim := func(obj interface{}) (interface{}, error) {\n601: \t\tif accessor, err := meta.Accessor(obj); err == nil {\n602: \t\t\tif accessor.GetManagedFields() != nil {\n603: \t\t\t\taccessor.SetManagedFields(nil)\n604: \t\t\t}\n605: \t\t}\n606: \t\treturn obj, nil\n607: \t}\n608: \n609: \tversionedClient := \n612: \tmetadataClient := metadata.NewForConfigOrDie(rootClientBuilder.ConfigOrDie(\"metadata-informers\"))\n613: \tmetadataInformers := metadatainformer.NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions(metadataClient, ResyncPeriod(s)(), metadatainformer.WithTransform(trim))\n614: \n615: \t// If apiserver is not running we should wait for some time and fail only then. This is particularly\n616: \t// important when we start apiserver and controller manager at the same time.\n617: \tif err := genericcontrollermanager.WaitForAPIServer(versionedClient, 10*time.Second); err != nil {\n618: \t\treturn ControllerContext{}, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to wait for apiserver being healthy: %v\", err)\n619: \t}\n620: \n621: \t// Use a discovery client capable of being refreshed.\n622: \tdiscoveryClient := rootClientBuilder.DiscoveryClientOrDie(\"controller-discovery\")\n623: \tcachedClient := cacheddiscovery.NewMemCacheClient(discoveryClient)\n624: \trestMapper := restmapper.NewDeferredDiscoveryRESTMapper(cachedClient)\n625: \tgo wait.Until(func() {\n626: \t\trestMapper.Reset()\n627: \t}, 30*time.Second, ctx.Done())\n628: \n629: \tcontrollerContext := ControllerContext{\n630: \t\tClientBuilder:                   clientBuilder,\n631: \t\tInformerFactory:                 sharedInformers,\n632: \t\tObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory: informerfactory.NewInformerFactory(sharedInformers, metadataInformers),\n633: \t\tComponentConfig:                 s.ComponentConfig,\n634: \t\tRESTMapper:                      restMapper,\n635: \t\tInformersStarted:                make(chan struct{}),\n636: \t\tResyncPeriod:                    ResyncPeriod(s),\n637: \t\tControllerManagerMetrics:        controllersmetrics.NewControllerManagerMetrics(\"kube-controller-manager\"),\n638: \t}\n639: \n640: \tif controllerContext.ComponentConfig.GarbageCollectorController.EnableGarbageCollector &&\n641: \t\tcontrollerContext.IsControllerEnabled(NewControllerDescriptors()[names.GarbageCollectorController]) {\n642: \t\tignoredResources := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n643: \t\tfor _, r := \t\t\tignoredResources,\n652: \t\t\tcontrollerContext.ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory,\n653: \t\t\tcontrollerContext.InformersStarted,\n654: \t\t)\n655: \t}\n656: \n657: \tcontrollersmetrics.Register()\n658: \treturn controllerContext, nil\n659: }\n660: \n661: // StartControllers starts a set of controllers with a specified ControllerContext\n662: func StartControllers(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptors map[string]*ControllerDescriptor,\n663: \tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux, healthzHandler *controllerhealthz.MutableHealthzHandler) error {\n664: \tvar controllerChecks []healthz.HealthChecker\n665: \n666: \t// Always start the SA token controller first using a full-power client, since it needs to mint tokens for the rest\n667: \t// If this fails, just return here and fail since other controllers won't be able to get credentials.\n668: \tif serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, ok := controllerDescriptors[names.ServiceAccountTokenController]; ok {\n669: \t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, serviceAccountTokenControllerDescriptor, unsecuredMux)\n670: \t\tif err != nil {\n671: \t\t\treturn err\n672: \t\t}\n673: \t\tif check != nil {\n674: \t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n675: \t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n676: \t\t}\n677: \t}\n678: \n679: \t// Each controller is passed a context where the logger has the name of\n680: \t// the controller set through WithName. That name then becomes the prefix of\n681: \t// of all log messages emitted by that controller.\n682: \t//\n683: \t// In StartController, an explicit \"controller\" key is used instead, for two reasons:\n684: \t// - while contextual logging is alpha, klog.LoggerWithName is still a no-op,\n685: \t//   so we cannot rely on it yet to add the name\n686: \t// - it allows distinguishing between log entries emitted by the controller\n687: \t//   and those emitted for it - this is a bit debatable and could be revised.\n688: \tfor _, controllerDesc := range controllerDescriptors {\n689: \t\tif controllerDesc.RequiresSpecialHandling() {\n690: \t\t\tcontinue\n691: \t\t}\n692: \n693: \t\tcheck, err := StartController(ctx, controllerCtx, controllerDesc, unsecuredMux)\n694: \t\tif err != nil {\n695: \t\t\treturn err\n696: \t\t}\n697: \t\tif check != nil {\n698: \t\t\t// HealthChecker should be present when controller has started\n699: \t\t\tcontrollerChecks = append(controllerChecks, check)\n700: \t\t}\n701: \t}\n702: \n703: \thealthzHandler.AddHealthChecker(controllerChecks...)\n704: \n705: \treturn nil\n706: }\n707: \n708: // StartController starts a controller with a specified ControllerContext\n709: // and performs required pre- and post- checks/actions\n710: func StartController(ctx context.Context, controllerCtx ControllerContext, controllerDescriptor *ControllerDescriptor,\n711: \tunsecuredMux *mux.PathRecorderMux) (healthz.HealthChecker, error) {\n712: \tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n713: \tcontrollerName := controllerDescriptor.Name()\n714: \n715: \tfor _, featureGate := range controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates() {\n716: \t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(featureGate) {\n717: \t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Controller is disabled by a feature gate\", \"controller\", controllerName, \"requiredFeatureGates\", controllerDescriptor.GetRequiredFeatureGates())\n718: \t\t\treturn nil, nil\n719: \t\t}\n720: \t}\n721: \n722: \tif controllerDescriptor.IsCloudProviderController() {\n723: \t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping a cloud provider controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n724: \t\treturn nil, nil\n725: \t}\n726: \n727: \tif !controllerCtx.IsControllerEnabled(controllerDescriptor) {\n728: \t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: controller is disabled\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n729: \t\treturn nil, nil\n730: \t}\n731: \n732: \ttime.Sleep(wait.Jitter(controllerCtx.ComponentConfig.Generic.ControllerStartInterval.Duration, ControllerStartJitter))\n733: \n734: \tlogger.V(1).Info(\"Starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n735: \n736: \tinitFunc := controllerDescriptor.GetInitFunc()\n737: \tctrl, started, err := initFunc(klog.NewContext(ctx, klog.LoggerWithName(logger, controllerName)), controllerCtx, controllerName)\n738: \tif err != nil {\n739: \t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error starting controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n740: \t\treturn nil, err\n741: \t}\n742: \tif !started {\n743: \t\tlogger.Info(\"Warning: skipping controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n744: \t\treturn nil, nil\n745: \t}\n746: \n747: \tcheck := controllerhealthz.NamedPingChecker(controllerName)\n748: \tif ctrl != nil {\n749: \t\t// check if the controller supports and requests a debugHandler\n750: \t\t// and it needs the unsecuredMux to mount the handler onto.\n751: \t\tif debuggable, ok := ctrl.(controller.Debuggable); ok && unsecuredMux != nil {\n752: \t\t\tif debugHandler := debuggable.DebuggingHandler(); debugHandler != nil {\n753: \t\t\t\tbasePath := \"/debug/controllers/\" + controllerName\n754: \t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandle(basePath, http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n755: \t\t\t\tunsecuredMux.UnlistedHandlePrefix(basePath+\"/\", http.StripPrefix(basePath, debugHandler))\n756: \t\t\t}\n757: \t\t}\n758: \t\tif healthCheckable, ok := ctrl.(controller.HealthCheckable); ok {\n759: \t\t\tif realCheck := healthCheckable.HealthChecker(); realCheck != nil {\n760: \t\t\t\tcheck = controllerhealthz.NamedHealthChecker(controllerName, realCheck)\n761: \t\t\t}\n762: \t\t}\n763: \t}\n764: \n765: \tlogger.Info(\"Started controller\", \"controller\", controllerName)\n766: \treturn check, nil\n767: }\n768: \n769: // serviceAccountTokenControllerStarter is special because it must run first to set up permissions for other controllers.\n770: // It kubernetes/kubernetes, controllers register themselves with the controller manager through a descriptor-based initialization pattern rather than the `SetupWithManager` pattern used in controller-runtime.\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. **ControllerDescriptor** (controllermanager.go:421-429)\\nDescribes a controller with metadata including:\\n- `name`: Controller identifier\\n- `initFunc`: Function that initializes and starts the controller\\n- `aliases`: Backward-compatible names\\n- `requiredFeatureGates`: Feature gates needed\\n- `isDisabledByDefault`: Whether the controller is disabled by default\\n- `isCloudProviderController`: Whether this is a cloud provider-specific controller\\n\\n### 2. **InitFunc Type** (controllermanager.go:419)\\n```go\\ntype InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)\\n```\\nThe InitFunc is the equivalent of `SetupWithManager` - it's responsible for:\\n- Creating the controller instance\\n- Configuring event handlers and informers\\n- Starting the controller's reconciliation loop\\n- Returning whether the controller was enabled and any errors\\n\\n### 3. **ControllerContext** (controllermanager.go:366-401)\\nProvides controllers with necessary resources:\\n- `ClientBuilder`: For creating API clients\\n- `InformerFactory`: For creating informers to watch Kubernetes resources\\n- `ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory`: For watching typed and dynamic resources\\n- `ComponentConfig`: Controller-specific configuration\\n- `RESTMapper`: For mapping resources to REST endpoints\\n- `InformersStarted`: Channel signaling when informers have started\\n- `ResyncPeriod`: Function generating periodic resync intervals\\n- `ControllerManagerMetrics`: For tracking controller metrics\\n- `GraphBuilder`: For garbage collector dependency tracking\\n\\n### 4. **controller.Interface** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go:25-55)\\nThe base interface that all controllers must implement:\\n- `Name() string`: Returns the controller's canonical name\\n- Optional `Debuggable` interface: Provides debugging HTTP handlers\\n- Optional `HealthCheckable` interface: Provides health check endpoints\\n\\n## Controller Registration Flow\\n\\n### Step 1: Descriptor Definition\\nEach controller is defined through a `newXxxControllerDescriptor()` function. For example, in core.go:\\n```go\\nfunc newEndpointsControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n    return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n        name:     names.EndpointsController,\\n        aliases:  []string{\\\"endpoint\\\"},\\n        initFunc: startEndpointsController,\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Step 2: Controller Initialization\\nThe `initFunc` (e.g., `startEndpointsController`) is called to initialize the controller:\\n```go\\nfunc startEndpointsController(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {\\n    go endpointcontroller.NewEndpointController(\\n        ctx,\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Pods(),\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Services(),\\n        controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Endpoints(),\\n        controllerContext.ClientBuilder.ClientOrDie(\\\"endpoint-controller\\\"),\\n        controllerContext.ComponentConfig.EndpointController.EndpointUpdatesBatchPeriod.Duration,\\n    ).Run(ctx, int(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.EndpointController.ConcurrentEndpointSyncs))\\n    return nil, true, nil\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Step 3: Manager Registration\\nControllers are registered in `NewControllerDescriptors()` (controllermanager.go:495-593):\\n```go\\nregister(newEndpointsControllerDescriptor())\\nregister(newEndpointSliceControllerDescriptor())\\n// ... more controller registrations\\n```\\n\\n### Step 4: Starting Controllers\\nThe `StartControllers()` function (controllermanager.go:662-706) iterates through registered controllers and calls `StartController()` for each.\\n\\n`StartController()` (controllermanager.go:708-767):\\n- Checks if controller is enabled\\n- Calls the controller's `InitFunc`\\n- Registers health checkers\\n- Mounts any debugging handlers\\n\\n## Reconciliation Pattern\\n\\nKubernetes controllers use the **Reconciler** pattern internally for state reconciliation. Examples include:\\n\\n### Volume Manager Reconciler (pkg/kubelet/volumemanager/reconciler/reconciler_common.go:49-51)\\n```go\\ntype Reconciler interface {\\n    Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\\n    if volumes that should be mounted are mounted and volumes that should\\n    not be mounted are unmounted.\\n    Run(stopCh <-chan struct{})\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Plugin Manager Reconciler (pkg/kubelet/pluginmanager/reconciler/reconciler.go:37-41)\\n```go\\ntype Reconciler interface {\\n    Run starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically,\\n    checks if plugins are correctly registered or unregistered.\\n    Run(stopCh <-chan struct{})\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Attach/Detach Controller Reconciler (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go:301-305)\\nThe attach/detach controller uses a reconciler to periodically reconcile the desired and actual state of volume attachments:\\n```go\\nreconciler reconciler.Reconciler\\n```\\n\\n## Key Differences from controller-runtime\\n\\nWhile the Kubernetes native controllers don't use the `SetupWithManager` pattern from controller-runtime, they achieve the same goals through:\\n\\n1. **ControllerDescriptor** instead of SetupWithManager: Encapsulates controller metadata and initialization logic\\n2. **InitFunc** instead of imperative setup: Declarative function that returns the initialized controller\\n3. **ControllerContext** instead of Manager: Provides all necessary dependencies and resources\\n4. **controller.Interface** instead of reconciler.Reconciler: Base interface for all controller types\\n5. **Explicit Manager Loop**: The `Run()` function in controllermanager.go orchestrates controller startup and lifecycle\\n\\nThis design allows Kubernetes to manage many heterogeneous controllers with different initialization patterns and dependencies while maintaining a consistent registration and lifecycle management
